 dow

 15 varsh tak kii umr ke bachche is beemaari kii chapet main aa rahe hai

 Bihar: 31 children have died in Muzaffarpur reportedly due to Acute Encephalitis Syndrome (AES)

 uski paribhaasha alag thi

 hero or villen kaa antar dekhnaa dilachasp he

 unka apana group or power hoti he

 yahi donon main sabase bada antar hota he

 After the passage of this bill in Parliament, professional surrogacy cannot be done for professional money only
 It is only for the needy infertile couples to be approved as morally surrogate mother
 sarkaar ke is faisle par chautarafa bahes bhi chhid gai he jisame is baat par sawaal uth rahe hai ki kya ye faisla sarkaar kii vichaardhaara yaa soch he yaa phir samaaj kii jarurat

 Which happens to the biological child
 unhone kaha ki serogesi kaa ismetal aniatik tareeke se kiya jane laga he jise rokna he or nayaa bill usamen madad karegaa

 saroget maa board kaa gathan hogaane kanoonon kaa thik se paalan ho sake uske liye kendriya str par, rajyon or centre shasit rajyon main bhi saroget maa board kaa gathan kiya jayega

 sarkaar ne bill ke paksh main jo daleel di wo he ki pichley kuch saal se bharat ko ‘sarogesi hub’ kaha jane laga tha
 Because there was a low cost of rent here
 rural or tribal mahilaon kaa khaas taur par shoshan ho rahaa tha
 The previous governments promised to introduce the bill in Parliament 11 times but did not fulfill it
 koun nahin le sakenge sarogesi kaa sahaara?single pareint, liv-in couples, homosexual couples or anamarid couples

 Provision of punishment for breaking the rules will be imprisoned for 10 years for breaking the new rules of surrogacy and a fine of up to Rs 10 lakh
 bachche ko chhodana or commercial sarogesi gaiyr kanoonee maane gaye hai

 The Election Commission has recommended in a letter to the Central Government that there should be a provision for disqualifying the mlas or mps against whom they have filed chargesheet in the case of bribing voters in the election
 ayog ke ucch padasth sutron ke mutabik kanoon mantralay ko bheje patr main ayog ne likhaa he ki iske liye jan pratinidhitiv kanoon kii dhara 8 main sanshodhan karke is praavdhaan joda jaae
 According to the current provision of the Representation of the People Act, if a criminal offense is proved against the public representative and when he is sentenced, then he is banned from the post after the completion of the term of the sentence and contesting the election till 6 years after that
 adaalat main tay hone vaale aaropon main sazaa kam se kam paanch saal tak kii ho

 The Law Commission believes that these provisions are not sufficient to prevent criminalization of politics
 kyonki kanoonee maamalon lambey vakt chalane or bahum kam maamalon main sajaa sunai jaati he
 But the Election Commission wants that the public representative should be disqualified even on bribe and illegitimate pressure in the election
 chunaav ayog kaa kahana he ki matadaata ko rishwat dena ek gambhir aparaadh he or isse sakhti se nipta janaa chahie
 This recommendation of the Election Commission has come in the wake of complaints of corruption in elections in recent years, where many complaints have been received for exchange of notes
 chunaav ayukta naseem jaidi pehle janpratinidhi kanoon kii dhara 58A main sanshodhan karne kii maang kar chuke hai jo booth capcharing ke maamle main chunaav radd yaa sthagit karne kaa samarthan karata he
